```

Launch Steam Launching Steam... ```python
import os
import subprocess
import string
def launch_program():
    program_relative_path = 'Program Files (x86)\\Steam\\Steam.exe'
    for drive in string.ascii_uppercase:
        full_path = f'{drive}:\\{program_relative_path}'
        if os.path.exists(full_path):
            subprocess.Popen(full_path)
            return
    print('Steam.exe not found in expected directories.')
if __name__ == '__main__':
    launch_program()
```

Play {music_name} Playing {music_name}... ```python
from youtubesearchpython import VideosSearch
import re, webbrowser
def play_youtube(query):
    music = VideosSearch(query, limit=15).result()['result']
    music_video = sorted(music, key=lambda video: int(re.sub('[^0-9]', '', video['viewCount']['text'] or '0')))
    if music_video: webbrowser.open(music_video[-1]['link'])
if __name__ == '__main__':
    play_youtube('{music_name}')
```

Play what is love Playing what is love... ```python
from youtubesearchpython import VideosSearch
import re, webbrowser
def play_youtube(query):
    music = VideosSearch('what is love', limit=15).result()['result'] #'result' is a key
    music_video = sorted(music, key=lambda video: int(re.sub('[^0-9]', '', video['viewCount']['text'] or '0'))) # viewCount is only correct form
    if music_video: webbrowser.open(music_video[-1]['link']) #'link' is a key
if __name__ == '__main__':
    play_youtube('what is love')
```

Display the top 10 news from Poland Displaying the top 10 news from Poland... ```python
import requests as r
u = 'https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines?country=PL&apiKey=870428dbdb2940d2a52a3ebe2d8c3645'
j = r.get(u).json()
a = j.get('articles', [])
if a:
    print('Top 10 News:')
    for i, t in enumerate(a[:10]):
        print(f'{i+1}. {t.get('title', 'No title')}')
else:
    print('No news or unexpected API response.')
```

Track for new Gmail messages Tracking for new Gmail messages... ```python
import imaplib
mail = imaplib.IMAP4_SSL('imap.gmail.com')
mail.login('your_email@gmail.com', 'your_password')
mail.select('inbox')
type, data = mail.search(None, 'UNSEEN')
unseen_count = len(data[0].split())
print(f'You have {unseen_count} unread messages.')
```

Check my FPS Checking your FPS... ```python
import time
def check_fps():
    t1, cnt, intv = time.time(), 0, 1
    nxt = t1 + intv
    while True:
        cnt += 1
        time.sleep(0.001)
        t2 = time.time()
        if t2 >= nxt:
            print(f'FPS: {cnt / intv}')
            cnt, t1 = 0, t2
            nxt = t2 + intv
if __name__ == '__main__':
    check_fps()
```

Check FPS Checking FPS... ```python

def check_fps():

if __name__ == '__main__':
    check_fps()

Can you check FPS? Sure! Checking FPS... ```python
import time
def check_fps():
    t1, cnt, intv = time.time(), 0, 1
    nxt = t1 + intv
    while True:
        cnt += 1
        time.sleep(0.001)
        t2 = time.time()
        if t2 >= nxt:
            print(f'FPS: {cnt / intv}')
            cnt, t1 = 0, t2
            nxt = t2 + intv
if __name__ == '__main__':
    check_fps()
```

Check GPU usage Checking GPU usage... ```python

    print(f'GPU Usage (ID {gpu.id}): {gpu.load * 100}%')
```

Check the usage Checking the usage of CPU, RAM, Disk, and GPU... ```python
import psutil
# CPU usage
cpu_usage = psutil.cpu_percent()
# RAM usage
ram_usage = psutil.virtual_memory().percent
# Disk usage
disk_usage = psutil.disk_usage('/').percent
print(f'CPU Usage: {cpu_usage}%')
print(f'RAM Usage: {ram_usage}%')
print(f'Disk Usage: {disk_usage}%')
```

Check hardware usage Checking the usage of CPU, RAM, Disk, and GPU... ```python
import psutil
# CPU usage
cpu_usage = psutil.cpu_percent()
# RAM usage
ram_usage = psutil.virtual_memory().percent
# Disk usage
disk_usage = psutil.disk_usage('/').percent
print(f'CPU Usage: {cpu_usage}%')
print(f'RAM Usage: {ram_usage}%')
print(f'Disk Usage: {disk_usage}%')

Mark all messages as seen Marking all Gmail messages as seen... ```python
import imaplib
mail = imaplib.IMAP4_SSL('imap.gmail.com')
mail.login('your_email@gmail.com', 'your_password')
mail.select('inbox')
mail.store('1:*', '+FLAGS', '(\Seen)')
print('All messages marked as seen.')
```

Remove latest message Removing the latest Gmail message... ```python
import imaplib
mail = imaplib.IMAP4_SSL('imap.gmail.com')
mail.login('your_email@gmail.com', 'your_password')
mail.select('inbox')
type, data = mail.search(None, 'ALL')
mail_ids = data[0]
id_list = mail_ids.split()
latest_email_id = id_list[-1]
mail.store(latest_email_id, '+FLAGS', '(\Deleted)')
mail.expunge()
print('Latest message deleted.')
```

Check weather outside Checking weather outside... ```python
import requests
import geocoder
def get_weather():
    g = geocoder.ip('me')
    latlng = g.latlng
    lat, lon = latlng[0], latlng[1]
    r = requests.get(f'http://api.weatherapi.com/v1/current.json?key=asdgfgdfsg241412sa&q={lat},{lon}')
    d = r.json()['current']
    print(f"{d['condition']['text']} {d['temp_c']}?C {d['wind_kph']}kph {d['humidity']}%")
get_weather()
```

Predict my location Predicting your location... ```python
import geocoder
def predict_location():

Geocode New York Geocoding the location name 'New York'... ```python
import geocoder
def geocode_location(location):
    g = geocoder.osm(location)
    print(g.latlng)
geocode_location('New York')
```

Reverse geocode 40.7128, -74.0060 Reverse geocoding the coordinates 40.7128, -74.0060... ```python
import geocoder
def reverse_geocode(lat, lon):
    g = geocoder.osm([lat, lon], method='reverse')
    print(g.address)
reverse_geocode(40.7128, -74.0060)
```

Send an email {contents} to {email} Sending an email to {email}... ```python

server.sendmail('from_email@gmail.com', 'to_email@gmail.com', 'contents')
server.quit()
```

Record 5 seconds long audio Recording audio for 5 seconds... ```python
import sounddevice as sd
import numpy as np
import wavio
duration = 5  # seconds
rate = 44100  # samples per second
sd.default.samplerate = rate
sd.default.channels = 2
audio_data = sd.rec(int(rate * duration))
sd.wait()
wavio.write('audio.wav', audio_data, rate, sampwidth=2)
```

Solve the quadratic equation \( ax^2 + bx + c = 0 \) Solving the quadratic equation... ```python
import cmath
a, b, c = 1, -3, 2
root1 = (-b + cmath.sqrt(b**2 - 4*a*c)) / (2 * a)
root2 = (-b - cmath.sqrt(b**2 - 4*a*c)) / (2 * a)
print(f'Roots are {root1} and {root2}')
```

Find the derivative of \( f(x) = x^2 \) Finding the derivative of the function... ```python
from sympy import symbols, diff
x = symbols('x')
f = x ** 2
derivative = diff(f, x)
print(f'Derivative of f(x) is {derivative}')
```

```

Find the limit of \( f(x) = x^2 \) as \( x \) approaches 2 Finding the limit... ```python
from sympy import symbols, limit
x = symbols('x')
f = x ** 2
lim = limit(f, x, 2)
print(f'The limit is {lim}')
```

Find the integral of \( f(x) = x^2 \) Finding the integral... ```python
from sympy import symbols, integrate
x = symbols('x')
f = x ** 2
integral = integrate(f, x)
print(f'Integral of f(x) is {integral}')
```

Solve the system of equations \( 2x + y = 8 \) and \( x - y = 4 \) Solving the system of equations... ```python
from sympy import symbols, Eq, solve
x, y = symbols('x y')
eq1 = Eq(2*x + y, 8)
eq2 = Eq(x - y, 4)
solution = solve((eq1, eq2), (x, y))
print(f'Solution is {solution}')
```

Find the eigenvalues of the matrix \( A \) Finding the eigenvalues... ```python
import numpy as np
A = np.array([[4, 2], [1, 3]])

print(f'Eigenvalues are {eigenvalues}')

Connect to Bluetooth device Connecting to Bluetooth device... ```python
from pybluez import BluetoothSocket, RFCOMM, discover_devices
nearby_devices = discover_devices(lookup_names=True)
if nearby_devices:
    first_device_address = nearby_devices[0][0]
    sock = BluetoothSocket(RFCOMM)
    sock.connect((first_device_address, 1))
```

Close the Colaboratory tab in 1 hour Closing the Colaboratory tab scheduled to 1 hour... ```python
import time
from pygetwindow import getWindowsWithTitle
import pyautogui
scheduled_to = 3600 # 1h
time.sleep(scheduled_to)
windows = getWindowsWithTitle('Colaboratory')
if windows:
    target_window = windows[0]
    target_window.activate()
    time.sleep(2)
    pyautogui.moveTo(target_window.left + 200, target_window.top + 5)
    pyautogui.click()
    pyautogui.hotkey('ctrl', 'w')
    time.sleep(1)
    pyautogui.press('enter')
```

Volume down Decreasing volume... ```python
from ctypes import cast, POINTER
from comtypes import CLSCTX_ALL
from pycaw.pycaw import AudioUtilities, IAudioEndpointVolume
def main():
    devices = AudioUtilities.GetSpeakers()
    interface = devices.Activate(IAudioEndpointVolume._iid_, CLSCTX_ALL, None)
    volume = cast(interface, POINTER(IAudioEndpointVolume))
    current_volume = volume.GetMasterVolumeLevelScalar()
    new_volume = max(0.0, current_volume - 0.1)  # Decrease by 10%
    volume.SetMasterVolumeLevelScalar(new_volume, None)
if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

Increase volume Increasing volume... ```python
from ctypes import cast, POINTER
from comtypes import CLSCTX_ALL
from pycaw.pycaw import AudioUtilities, IAudioEndpointVolume
def main():
    devices = AudioUtilities.GetSpeakers()
    interface = devices.Activate(IAudioEndpointVolume._iid_, CLSCTX_ALL, None)
    volume = cast(interface, POINTER(IAudioEndpointVolume))
    current_volume = volume.GetMasterVolumeLevelScalar()
    new_volume = min(1.0, current_volume + 0.1)  # Increase by 10%
    volume.SetMasterVolumeLevelScalar(new_volume, None)
if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

Show current volume level Displaying current volume level... ```python
from ctypes import cast, POINTER
from comtypes import CLSCTX_ALL
from pycaw.pycaw import AudioUtilities, IAudioEndpointVolume
def main():
    devices = AudioUtilities.GetSpeakers()
    interface = devices.Activate(IAudioEndpointVolume._iid_, CLSCTX_ALL, None)
    volume = cast(interface, POINTER(IAudioEndpointVolume))
    current_volume = volume.GetMasterVolumeLevelScalar()
    print(f'Current volume level is {current_volume * 100}%')
if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

Add file.exe to exclusion from Defender and incoming and outgoing firewall rules Adding file.exe to exclusions and setting up firewall rules... ```python
import subprocess
# Add to Windows Defender exclusion list
subprocess.run(['powershell', 'Add-MpPreference', '-ExclusionPath', 'path\to\file.exe'])
# Add to Windows Firewall for incoming and outgoing rules
subprocess.run(['netsh', 'advfirewall', 'firewall', 'add', 'rule', 'name=Incoming File Exclusion', 'dir=in', 'action=allow', 'program=path\to\file.exe'])
subprocess.run(['netsh', 'advfirewall', 'firewall', 'add', 'rule', 'name=Outgoing File Exclusion', 'dir=out', 'action=allow', 'program=path\to\file.exe'])
```
